<p>The Free Fire Advance Server is a testing ground for the Free Fire game. It mutually benefits the developers and the players. The players not only enjoy features that are not yet available to the general player base, but also have the power to influence the overall development process of the game.</p>



<p>The players are expected to share their thoughts on how the game can be improved. Besides that they are also expected to look for and report bugs and glitches in the <strong>Advance Server</strong> so that they can be fixed before launch to the general player base.</p>



<p>The developers get valuable feedback and bug reports so that they can work on fixing bugs and improving the quality of the game. This way it mutually benefits both the developers and players.</p>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-3 kt-pane11_fd87ca-0b"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">How often do the advance server updates come?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Developers launch it every 2 months, typically 1 to 2 weeks ahead of the official launch. The main purpose of Advance Server is to provide a real life experimental ground to test its updates.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-4 kt-pane11_52ceb5-e5"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Can anyone access the Free Fire Advance Server APK?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>No, the FF Advance Server is only accessible to registered users. Always use official channels. Using unauthorized methods can result in the termination of accounts.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-5 kt-pane11_e32de0-1b"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">What do I get, if I report bugs and glitches in the FF Advance Server?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Reporting bugs and glitches is a great way to earn amazing rewards including diamonds and skins.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-6 kt-pane11_c07ae6-7b"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Is there any risk involved with the Free Fire Advance Server?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>If you strictly follow official channels and don’t violate the terms and conditions. The FF advance Server is a very safe platform with no risks.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-7 kt-pane11_219cc1-29"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">What is the official website for the Free Fire Advance Server?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">

</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-8 kt-pane11_d44703-86"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">What does an activation code do in the Free Fire Advance Server?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>This is a unique code for each user that grants access to the Free Fire Advance Server Account. This code should be kept secret as each code gives access to one account only.<br></p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-9 kt-pane11_2b5a03-10"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Can I participate in the Free Fire Advance Server from any country?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Yes, you can access the Free Fire Advance Server from any country. Garena often releases updates on the Indonesian servers first. So the users can also use VPNs for that purpose.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-10 kt-pane11_9a21f0-f1"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Is there a specific device requirement to access the Free Fire Advance Server?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Since it is a test server, it often has unoptimized features. It is always better if your device has higher specifications for it to run smoothly.<br></p>
